Introduction

This documentation aims to provide all the information you need to work with our API.

As you scroll, you'll see code examples for working with the API in different programming languages in the dark area to the right (or as part of the content on mobile). You can switch the language used with the tabs at the top right (or from the nav menu at the top left on mobile).

Base URL

https://vast-plains-50606-af0454c6736c.herokuapp.com

Authenticating requests

This API is not authenticated.

Endpoints

POST api/register

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "https://vast-plains-50606-af0454c6736c.herokuapp.com/api/register" \
    --header "Authorization: Bearer eyJ0eXAiOiJKV1QiLCJhbGciOiJSUzI1NiJ9.eyJhdWQiOiIxIiwianRpIjoiNjI5ODc4ODRjMzhhYmI0YWVlODMzYzllZmJjNWM4Nzk5M2U4OWFhNzg2MWE4YTNjN2Q4NjBhMWE0MzljZjFkZTM3NGQ0ODZhMDZkZWQ3MGMiLCJpYXQiOjE3MDc4MDU1NTQuNDA4NTk3LCJuYmYiOjE3MDc4MDU1NTQuNDA4NTk4LCJleHAiOjE3Mzk0Mjc5NTMuNzY1OTQsInN1YiI6IjIiLCJzY29wZXMiOlsiKiJdfQ.AnxvaQhezFODdQ1Cbv32MbyJe48dyoY_zECs2cPdZSSi-G2mwns1GRUrVDarfXrof4axI0iHjVkwVGI_1cjRRf2VJIe3_JBRFyocxrzyNMFaGd1HzFJD9VjONAme5p4FELZ_g0cAcQ24VB-Am4JtDyiK0Mh8yR-mvzF7Dl76Yrnc36ymR2dEtw16HPIw2dZ8dT3ALn9kw51xoQd3VrEftYUSGFjvLHF_pieL2uXe4L7uGbP0ue_QuTpiD9iXXgcq2FITd-GCUJHYs3sZCkj2ds6q_5CVfSsaPq409bydNsBMfQ4AYE3_0hcn5y8-eCz2AL0-mMKcDVNu_mDj3PlprCu6vLXcvrNRDs0G4fRh-pHT-yiiH8boe1fBV7-UrJNT_FHCyf5-szgWHXST7WO7OVXNs4nS7V2DFtj3ih-cOkSWQQZ18-bX8v-vR_9vwTWsqFF6VO9wseBoEgOF8P7TpHubnCtf6ykmij8b85eJGsToTZoSc-5hyh_NsJXO9CzCma3uAOj7_EX-iRuAfWUQnOhhlP80iTyFcGXv3qwFei_tlH7d5rIhe7zgUUHXZr3i94F64s3iVCHIt8nb7k09_Zg5Y9rg2QorAzx5-eRdQhcGKMB3UGKt8zZXwN581r8oSPpo8xoJ_AEK8efybfuVqONewYSltVWSnLxIGlKwqBk" \

    \"email\": \"hillard08@example.org\",
    \"password\": \"qxa\"
}"

    "https://vast-plains-50606-af0454c6736c.herokuapp.com/api/register"
);

const headers = {
    "Authorization": "Bearer eyJ0eXAiOiJKV1QiLCJhbGciOiJSUzI1NiJ9.eyJhdWQiOiIxIiwianRpIjoiNjI5ODc4ODRjMzhhYmI0YWVlODMzYzllZmJjNWM4Nzk5M2U4OWFhNzg2MWE4YTNjN2Q4NjBhMWE0MzljZjFkZTM3NGQ0ODZhMDZkZWQ3MGMiLCJpYXQiOjE3MDc4MDU1NTQuNDA4NTk3LCJuYmYiOjE3MDc4MDU1NTQuNDA4NTk4LCJleHAiOjE3Mzk0Mjc5NTMuNzY1OTQsInN1YiI6IjIiLCJzY29wZXMiOlsiKiJdfQ.AnxvaQhezFODdQ1Cbv32MbyJe48dyoY_zECs2cPdZSSi-G2mwns1GRUrVDarfXrof4axI0iHjVkwVGI_1cjRRf2VJIe3_JBRFyocxrzyNMFaGd1HzFJD9VjONAme5p4FELZ_g0cAcQ24VB-Am4JtDyiK0Mh8yR-mvzF7Dl76Yrnc36ymR2dEtw16HPIw2dZ8dT3ALn9kw51xoQd3VrEftYUSGFjvLHF_pieL2uXe4L7uGbP0ue_QuTpiD9iXXgcq2FITd-GCUJHYs3sZCkj2ds6q_5CVfSsaPq409bydNsBMfQ4AYE3_0hcn5y8-eCz2AL0-mMKcDVNu_mDj3PlprCu6vLXcvrNRDs0G4fRh-pHT-yiiH8boe1fBV7-UrJNT_FHCyf5-szgWHXST7WO7OVXNs4nS7V2DFtj3ih-cOkSWQQZ18-bX8v-vR_9vwTWsqFF6VO9wseBoEgOF8P7TpHubnCtf6ykmij8b85eJGsToTZoSc-5hyh_NsJXO9CzCma3uAOj7_EX-iRuAfWUQnOhhlP80iTyFcGXv3qwFei_tlH7d5rIhe7zgUUHXZr3i94F64s3iVCHIt8nb7k09_Zg5Y9rg2QorAzx5-eRdQhcGKMB3UGKt8zZXwN581r8oSPpo8xoJ_AEK8efybfuVqONewYSltVWSnLxIGlKwqBk",

let body = {
    "name": "aliquam",
    "email": "hillard08@example.org",
    "password": "qxa"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());

POST api/register

Body Parameters

name  string  

email  string  

Must be a valid email address.

password  string  

Must be at least 6 characters.

Request      

POST api/responses/batch

Body Parameters

responses  object[] optional  

responses[].survey_id  string  

responses[].question_id  string  

responses[].question_type  string  

Must be one of yes_no, open_ended, rating, or multiple_choice.

responses[].response_text  string optional  

This field is required when responses.*.question_type is open_ended.

responses[].rating_value  integer optional  

This field is required when responses.*.question_type is rating. Must be at least 1. Must not be greater than 5.

responses[].option_id  string optional  

This field is required when responses.*.question_type is yes_no.

responses[].options  string[] optional  

This field is required when responses.*.question_type is multiple_choice.
